0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.39628em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">e</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.26372em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ρ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f_i(\rho)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> 是第 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65952em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span></span> 个目标函数，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>k</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span></span> 是目标函数的数量。</p>
<p>多目标优化通常不存在单一的最优解，而是一组Pareto最优解，每个解在不同目标之间体现不同的权衡。</p>
<p>常见的多目标拓扑优化方法包括：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>加权和法</strong>：将多个目标函数线性组合为单一目标<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mrow><mi>w</mi><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>g</mi><mi>h</mi><mi>t</mi><mi>e</mi><mi>d</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ρ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>k</mi></munderover><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ρ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f_{weighted}(\rho) = \sum_{i=1}^{k} w_i f_i(\rho)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">h</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.11378em; vertical-align: -1.27767em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.83611em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.87233em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05001em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.30001em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.27767em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02691em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">w_i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02691em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是权重系数，满足 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>k</mi></msubsup><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sum_{i=1}^{k} w_i = 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.28872em; vertical-align: -0.29971em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="position: relative; top: -5e-06em;">∑</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.989008em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.40029em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2029em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.29971em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02691em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>。通过调整权重，可以得到Pareto前沿上的不同解。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>约束法</strong>：将一个目标作为优化目标，其他目标转化为约束条件<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><munder><mrow><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mi>ρ</mi></munder><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ρ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mtext>s.t.</mtext><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ρ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>ε</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>3</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mtext>其他约束</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\min_{\rho} \quad &amp; f_1(\rho) \\
\text{s.t.} \quad &amp; f_i(\rho) \leq \varepsilon_i, \quad i = 2, 3, \ldots, k \\
&amp; \text{其他约束}
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 4.97611em; vertical-align: -2.23805em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.73805em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.89805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.66786em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.4em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ρ</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">min</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.836108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.92195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">s.t.</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.42195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.23805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.73805em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.89805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.92195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ε</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.42195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord cjk_fallback">其他约束</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.23805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
通过调整约束值 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ε</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\varepsilon_i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ε</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>，可以探索不同的Pareto最优解。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>进化算法</strong>：如NSGA-II（非支配排序遗传算法）、MOEA/D（基于分解的多目标进化算法）等，能够同时生成多个Pareto最优解。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>目标规划法</strong>：设定每个目标的理想值，最小化实际值与理想值之间的偏差。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 id="单目标与多目标方法对比">单目标与多目标方法对比</h4>

<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>特性</th>
<th>单目标优化</th>
<th>多目标优化</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>目标函数</td>
<td>单一性能指标</td>
<td>多个性能指标</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>最优解</td>
<td>通常唯一</td>
<td>Pareto最优解集</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>计算复杂度</td>
<td>相对较低</td>
<td>较高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>决策过程</td>
<td>直接选择最优解</td>
<td>需要在Pareto解集中选择</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>适用场景</td>
<td>性能需求单一明确</td>
<td>多种性能需求并存</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>算法类型</td>
<td>梯度法为主</td>
<td>梯度法和启发式算法并用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table><p>在实际工程应用中，多目标拓扑优化更符合复杂机械结构的设计需求，但计算复杂度高、解集选择困难等问题限制了其应用。结合GNN与MORL的智能优化方法有望克服这些限制，提高多目标拓扑优化的效率和实用性。</p>
<h2 id="拓扑优化在工程中的应用">2.3.3 拓扑优化在工程中的应用</h2>
<p>拓扑优化已广泛应用于各种工程领域，推动了轻量化设计、高性能结构和创新形态的发展。主要应用领域包括：</p>
<h4 id="航空航天领域">航空航天领域</h4>
<p>在航空航天领域，拓扑优化用于设计轻量化结构组件，如机翼肋、发动机支架、卫星支撑结构等。通过减轻结构重量同时保持足够的强度和刚度，可以显著降低燃料消耗和提高飞行性能。例如，空客A380的机翼肋采用拓扑优化设计，减重约500kg。</p>
<h4 id="汽车工业">汽车工业</h4>
<p>汽车工业利用拓扑优化设计车身结构、底盘组件、悬挂系统等，以实现轻量化、提高安全性和改善NVH（噪声、振动与声振粗糙度）性能。宝马i8的车身结构和奔驰S级的发动机支架都采用了拓扑优化技术，实现了重量减轻15-25%的同时保持或提高了结构性能。</p>
<h4 id="医疗器械">医疗器械</h4>
<p>在医疗领域，拓扑优化用于设计定制化植入物（如髋关节、颅骨植入物）、假肢和医疗器械支架。这些优化设计不仅提高了力学性能，还改善了生物相容性和患者舒适度。</p>
<h4 id="建筑结构">建筑结构</h4>
<p>建筑领域应用拓扑优化设计桥梁、高层建筑支撑结构和特殊建筑形态。例如，卡塔尔多哈的托尔火炬塔和中国中央电视台总部大楼的结构设计都应用了拓扑优化原理。</p>
<h4 id="增材制造（3d打印）">增材制造（3D打印）</h4>
<p>拓扑优化与增材制造技术的结合，突破了传统制造工艺的限制，使复杂的优化结构能够被实际制造出来。这种结合促进了轻量化设计、功能集成和个性化定制的发展。</p>
<h4 id="热管理系统">热管理系统</h4>
<p>拓扑优化还应用于热管理系统设计，如散热器、热交换器等，通过优化材料分布提高热传导效率和均匀性。</p>
<h4 id="声学设计">声学设计</h4>
<p>在声学领域，拓扑优化用于设计消声器、声屏障和声学超材料，以实现特定的声学性能，如隔音、吸音或声波引导。</p>
<p>拓扑优化在工程应用中面临的主要挑战包括：</p>
<ul>
<li>制造约束的考虑（如最小特征尺寸、拔模角度等）</li>
<li>多物理场耦合问题的处理</li>
<li>计算效率与优化精度的平衡</li>
<li>优化结果的可解释性和工程实现</li>
</ul>
<p>结合人工智能技术的拓扑优化方法有望解决这些挑战，推动拓扑优化在更广泛工程领域的应用。</p>
<h2 id="多尺度建模与优化策略">2.4 多尺度建模与优化策略</h2>
<p>多尺度建模与优化是解决复杂机械结构设计问题的重要方法，它考虑了不同空间尺度上的结构特性和性能需求，从而实现更全面、更精确的结构优化。在机械结构设计中，多尺度问题普遍存在，如航空航天结构、复合材料、功能梯度材料等领域。</p>
<h2 id="多尺度建模的基本概念">2.4.1 多尺度建模的基本概念</h2>
<p>多尺度建模考虑结构在不同尺度层次上的行为和特性，通常包括以下三个主要尺度：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>宏观尺度（Macro-scale）</strong>：关注整体结构行为，尺寸通常在米或厘米级别，对应整个工程结构的全局性能，如整体刚度、强度、稳定性等。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>中观尺度（Meso-scale）</strong>：关注局部结构特征和组件级行为，尺寸通常在毫米级别，对应结构单元、连接部位、局部细节等。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>微观尺度（Micro-scale）</strong>：关注材料微结构和微观机理，尺寸通常在微米或纳米级别，对应材料晶粒、纤维排布、孔隙分布等微观特征。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>多尺度建模的核心思想是建立不同尺度之间的联系，实现信息在尺度间的传递和整合。这种方法能够捕获传统单尺度模型无法描述的复杂物理现象和结构行为。</p>
<h2 id="多尺度建模方法">2.4.2 多尺度建模方法</h2>
<p>多尺度建模方法主要包括以下几类：</p>
<h4 id="序列耦合方法">序列耦合方法</h4>
<p>序列耦合方法通过依次求解不同尺度的模型，并将一个尺度的计算结果作为另一个尺度的输入，实现尺度间的单向信息传递。其基本流程为：</p>
<ol>
<li>求解宏观模型，获取全局响应</li>
<li>将宏观响应作为边界条件应用于中观或微观模型</li>
<li>求解中观/微观模型，获取局部详细信息</li>
</ol>
<p>这种方法计算效率较高，但无法捕获尺度间的双向耦合效应。</p>
<h4 id="并行耦合方法">并行耦合方法</h4>
<p>并行耦合方法同时求解不同尺度的模型，并在求解过程中实现尺度间的双向信息交换。其数学表达可概括为：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>u</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">C</mi><mrow><mi>m</mi><mo>→</mo><mi>M</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>u</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>u</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">C</mi><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>→</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>u</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\mathcal{L}_M(u_M) &amp;= f_M + \mathcal{C}_{m\to M}(u_m) \\
\mathcal{L}_m(u_m) &amp;= f_m + \mathcal{C}_{M\to m}(u_M)
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3em; vertical-align: -1.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.75em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.91em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.25em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.75em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.91em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.05834em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.05834em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05834em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mrel mtight">→</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.25em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mi>M</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_m</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 分别是宏观和微观尺度的算子，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>u</mi><mi>M</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">u_M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>u</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">u_m</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是对应的解，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">C</mi><mrow><mi>m</mi><mo>→</mo><mi>M</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{C}_{m\to M}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.05834em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05834em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span><span class="mrel mtight">→</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">C</mi><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>→</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{C}_{M\to m}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.05834em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05834em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mrel mtight">→</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是尺度间的耦合算子。</p>
<p>并行耦合方法能够更准确地描述尺度间的相互作用，但计算复杂度高，实现难度大。</p>
<h4 id="均质化方法">均质化方法</h4>
<p>均质化方法是一种广泛应用的多尺度建模技术，通过求解代表性体积单元(RVE)的响应，推导等效宏观材料属性。其基本思想可表示为：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mi>j</mi><mi>k</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow><mrow><mi>e</mi><mi>f</mi><mi>f</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi>Y</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi></mrow></mfrac><msub><mo>∫</mo><mi>Y</mi></msub><msub><mi>C</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mi>j</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>n</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><msub><mi>δ</mi><mrow><mi>m</mi><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>δ</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow></msub><mo>−</mo><msubsup><mi>ε</mi><mrow><mi>m</mi><mi>n</mi></mrow><mrow><mi>k</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi>d</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{ijkl}^{eff} = \frac{1}{|Y|} \int_Y C_{ijmn}(y) \left(\delta_{mk}\delta_{nl} - \varepsilon_{mn}^{kl}(y)\right) dy</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.40443em; vertical-align: -0.437416em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.967016em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.39869em; margin-left: -0.07153em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">ijk</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">ff</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.437416em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.296em; vertical-align: -0.936em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.32144em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mord">∣</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.936em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol large-op" style="margin-right: 0.44445em; position: relative; top: -0.001125em;">∫</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist"><span class="" style="top: -1.78805em; margin-left: -0.44445em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.91195em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">mk</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03785em;">δ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ε</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.899108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">mn</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size1">)</span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mi>j</mi><mi>k</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow><mrow><mi>e</mi><mi>f</mi><mi>f</mi></mrow></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{ijkl}^{eff}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.40443em; vertical-align: -0.437416em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.967016em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.39869em; margin-left: -0.07153em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">ijk</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">ff</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.437416em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是均质化后的等效弹性张量，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mi>j</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>n</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{ijmn}(y)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.07153em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ijmn</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> 是微观尺度的局部弹性张量，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>ε</mi><mrow><mi>m</mi><mi>n</mi></mrow><mrow><mi>k</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\varepsilon_{mn}^{kl}(y)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ε</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">mn</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> 是特征应变场，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi>Y</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">|Y|</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mord">∣</span></span></span></span></span> 是RVE的体积。</p>
<p>均质化方法计算效率较高，适用于周期性微结构，但对非周期性结构和强非线性问题的处理能力有限。</p>
<h4 id="多重网格方法">多重网格方法</h4>
<p>多重网格方法使用不同分辨率的网格离散化结构，通过粗网格和细网格之间的信息传递，实现高效求解。其基本算法包括：</p>
<ol>
<li>在细网格上进行几次迭代，消除高频误差</li>
<li>将残差限制到粗网格上</li>
<li>在粗网格上求解误差方程</li>
<li>将粗网格解插值回细网格，修正细网格解</li>
<li>在细网格上进行几次平滑迭代</li>
</ol>
<p>多重网格方法计算效率高，收敛速度快，但实现复杂，对非结构化网格的适应性有限。</p>
<h2 id="多尺度优化策略">2.4.3 多尺度优化策略</h2>
<p>多尺度优化策略旨在同时或分阶段优化不同尺度上的结构特征，以实现整体性能的最优化。主要策略包括：</p>
<h4 id="分层优化策略">分层优化策略</h4>
<p>分层优化策略将多尺度优化问题分解为多个层次的子问题，按照从宏观到微观（或从微观到宏观）的顺序依次求解。其数学模型可表示为：</p>
<p><strong>宏观优化</strong>：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><munder><mrow><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub></munder><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msubsup><mi>P</mi><mi>m</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mtext>s.t.</mtext><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msubsup><mi>P</mi><mi>m</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mn>0</mn><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo>≤</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\min_{\rho_M} \quad &amp; f_M(\rho_M, P_m^*(\rho_M)) \\
\text{s.t.} \quad &amp; g_M(\rho_M, P_m^*(\rho_M)) \leq 0 \\
&amp; 0 \leq \rho_M \leq 1
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 4.97611em; vertical-align: -2.23805em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.73805em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.89805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.66786em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.4em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.35671em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143293em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">min</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.836108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.92195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">s.t.</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.42195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.23805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.73805em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.89805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em;
