margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">))</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.42195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.23805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong>微观优化</strong>：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msubsup><mi>P</mi><mi>m</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>arg</mi><mo>⁡</mo><munder><mrow><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></munder><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo separator="true">;</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mtext>s.t.</mtext><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo separator="true">;</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mn>0</mn><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo>≤</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
P_m^*(\rho_M) = \arg\min_{\rho_m} \quad &amp; f_m(\rho_m; \rho_M) \\
\text{s.t.} \quad &amp; g_m(\rho_m; \rho_M) \leq 0 \\
&amp; 0 \leq \rho_m \leq 1
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 4.97611em; vertical-align: -2.23805em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.73805em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.89805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.738696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mop">ar<span style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">g</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.66786em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.4em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.164543em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">min</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.836108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.92195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">s.t.</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.42195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.23805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.73805em;"><span class="" style="top: -4.89805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.92195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.42195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.23805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_m</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 分别是宏观和微观尺度的设计变量，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>P</mi><mi>m</mi><mo>∗</mo></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_m^*(\rho_M)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> 表示给定宏观设计下的最优微观参数。</p>
<p>分层优化策略计算效率较高，但可能无法找到全局最优解，因为它忽略了尺度间的完全耦合。</p>
<h4 id="并行优化策略">并行优化策略</h4>
<p>并行优化策略同时考虑多个尺度的优化目标，构建统一的优化问题：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><munder><mrow><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></mrow></munder><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mtext>s.t.</mtext><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mn>0</mn><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>M</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo>≤</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\min_{\rho_M, \rho_m} \quad &amp; w_M f_M(\rho_M, \rho_m) + w_m f_m(\rho_M, \rho_m) \\
\text{s.t.} \quad &amp; g_M(\rho_M, \rho_m) \leq 0 \\
&amp; g_m(\rho_M, \rho_m) \leq 0 \\
&amp; 0 \leq \rho_M, \rho_m \leq 1
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 6.47611em; vertical-align: -2.98805em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.48805em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.64805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.66786em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.4em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.35671em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143293em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.164543em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">min</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.836108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.67195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">s.t.</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.17195em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -0.671946em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.98805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.48805em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.64805em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02691em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -0.671946em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.98805em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>M</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">w_M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02691em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">w_m</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02691em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是权重系数，用于平衡不同尺度目标的重要性。</p>
<p>并行优化策略能够更全面地考虑尺度间的相互影响，但计算复杂度高，优化难度大。</p>
<h4 id="自适应优化策略">自适应优化策略</h4>
<p>自适应优化策略根据优化过程中的信息动态调整不同尺度的优化重点和计算资源分配。其基本流程包括：</p>
<ol>
<li>初始阶段以宏观优化为主</li>
<li>根据灵敏度分析识别关键区域</li>
<li>对关键区域进行细化建模和微观优化</li>
<li>更新宏观模型并继续优化</li>
<li>迭代上述过程直至收敛</li>
</ol>
<p>自适应优化策略能够平衡计算效率和优化质量，适用于复杂的工程问题。</p>
<h2 id="多尺度优化在机械结构中的应用">2.4.4 多尺度优化在机械结构中的应用</h2>
<p>多尺度优化在机械结构设计中有广泛的应用，主要包括：</p>
<h4 id="复合材料结构优化">复合材料结构优化</h4>
<p>复合材料结构涉及宏观层次的结构布局和微观层次的纤维排布、层合顺序等。多尺度优化可以同时优化这些不同尺度的设计参数，实现结构性能的最大化。</p>
<h4 id="功能梯度材料设计">功能梯度材料设计</h4>
<p>功能梯度材料(FGM)的性能取决于材料组分的空间分布。多尺度优化可以设计宏观的材料分布梯度和微观的材料界面结构，实现性能的定向调控。</p>
<h4 id="晶格结构设计">晶格结构设计</h4>
<p>晶格结构包含宏观的整体布局和微观的单元拓扑。多尺度优化可以同时优化这两个层次，设计出具有特定力学、热学或声学性能的轻量化结构。</p>
<h4 id="增材制造结构优化">增材制造结构优化</h4>
<p>增材制造技术能够实现复杂的多尺度结构。多尺度优化可以考虑宏观结构布局、中观支撑结构和微观打印参数，设计出既满足性能要求又适合增材制造的结构。</p>
<p>在本研究中将探索如何利用图神经网络和多目标强化学习技术，构建高效的多尺度拓扑优化框架，克服传统方法在计算效率和优化质量方面的局限。</p>
<h2 id="本章小结">2.5 本章小结</h2>
<p>本章介绍了基于GNN与MORL的机械结构拓扑优化所涉及的关键理论基础，包括图神经网络、多目标强化学习、拓扑优化以及多尺度建模与优化策略。</p>
<p>图神经网络作为一种处理非欧几里得数据的深度学习模型，能够有效捕获机械结构的拓扑关系和几何特征。GCN、GAT、GIN等不同类型的GNN模型各具特点，为结构特征提取和信息传递提供了多样化的技术选择。</p>
<p>多目标强化学习扩展了传统强化学习的框架，能够同时优化多个冲突的目标函数，为机械结构的多目标优化提供了新的解决思路。MORL通过不同的策略（如加权和法、Pareto前沿方法、策略集学习等）实现多目标之间的权衡与协调。</p>
<p>拓扑优化作为结构优化的重要方法，通过优化设计域内的材料分布，实现结构性能的最大化。单目标与多目标拓扑优化方法各有优缺点，在不同应用场景中发挥作用。拓扑优化已广泛应用于航空航天、汽车工业、医疗器械等多个工程领域。</p>
<p>多尺度建模与优化策略考虑了结构在不同空间尺度上的特性和行为，通过建立尺度间的联系，实现更全面、更精确的结构优化。分层优化、并行优化和自适应优化等不同策略适用于不同类型的多尺度问题。</p>
<p>这些理论基础为后续章节中基于GNN与MORL的拓扑优化算法设计提供了必要的知识支撑。通过将GNN的结构表示能力与MORL的多目标决策能力相结合，并考虑多尺度建模的思想，构建一个创新的机械结构拓扑优化框架，以克服传统方法的局限性，提高优化效率和结果质量。</p>
<h1 id="第三章-拓扑优化问题建模与图结构表示方法">第三章 拓扑优化问题建模与图结构表示方法</h1>
<h2 id="机械结构建模方法概述">3.1 机械结构建模方法概述</h2>
<p>机械结构的建模是拓扑优化的基础，它决定了优化问题的表达方式和求解策略。传统的机械结构建模方法主要基于有限元分析（FEA）框架，而本研究提出将图论与深度学习相结合的新型建模方法，以更好地适应复杂结构的表示需求。</p>
<h3 id="传统有限元建模方法">3.1.1 传统有限元建模方法</h3>
<p>有限元建模是结构分析和优化的经典方法，其基本思想是将连续的物理域离散为有限个单元，通过求解单元方程并组装得到整体结构的响应。在拓扑优化中，有限元建模通常包括以下步骤：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>几何建模</strong>：定义设计域的几何形状和边界</li>
<li><strong>网格划分</strong>：将设计域离散为有限个单元（如四边形、三角形、六面体等）</li>
<li><strong>材料属性定义</strong>：为每个单元分配材料属性（如杨氏模量、泊松比等）</li>
<li><strong>边界条件设置</strong>：定义位移约束、载荷条件等</li>
<li><strong>求解方程</strong>：建立并求解全局刚度方程 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>K</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Ku = F</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mord mathnormal">u</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ol>
<p>在拓扑优化中，设计变量通常是每个单元的材料密度 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>e</mi></msub><mo>∈</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_e \in [0,1]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.73354em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>，其中 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>e</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_e = 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span> 表示实体材料，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>e</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_e = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span> 表示空洞。材料属性与密度的关系通常采用SIMP（Solid Isotropic Material with Penalization）模型：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>E</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>e</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><msubsup><mi>ρ</mi><mi>e</mi><mi>p</mi></msubsup><msub><mi>E</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">E(\rho_e) = \rho_e^p E_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.961392em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.714392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">p</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>E</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">E_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是基础材料的杨氏模量，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span></span></span></span></span> 是惩罚因子（通常 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p &gt; 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.73354em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>）。</p>
<p>传统有限元建模方法的优点是理论成熟、计算精确，但在处理大规模、多尺度、多物理场耦合问题时计算效率低下，且难以捕获结构的拓扑特征和全局信息。</p>
<h3 id="基于图的结构建模方法">3.1.2 基于图的结构建模方法</h3>
<p>基于图的结构建模方法将机械结构表示为图 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>V</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>E</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G = (V, E)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>，其中节点集 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> 表示结构单元，边集 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>E</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">E</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span></span></span></span></span> 表示单元间的连接关系。这种表示方法具有以下优势：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>自然表达拓扑关系</strong>：图结构天然适合表示结构的拓扑连接关系</li>
<li><strong>多尺度表示能力</strong>：可通过层次化图结构表示不同尺度的特征</li>
<li><strong>计算效率高</strong>：图算法在处理大规模结构时具有较高的计算效率</li>
<li><strong>易于与深度学习结合</strong>：图神经网络可直接处理图结构数据</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="从网格到图：结构图构建策略">3.2 从网格到图：结构图构建策略</h2>
<p>将传统有限元网格转换为图结构是实现基于GNN的拓扑优化的关键步骤。本节提出一种系统的结构图构建策略，包括节点定义、边连接建立和特征赋值三个主要环节。</p>
<h3 id="节点定义策略">3.2.1 节点定义策略</h3>
<p>在结构图中，节点可以根据不同的建模需求进行定义。常见的节点定义策略包括：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>单元中心节点</strong>：每个有限元单元的中心作为图中的一个节点，适用于密度法拓扑优化</li>
<li><strong>网格节点</strong>：有限元网格的顶点作为图中的节点，适用于形状优化和边界演化</li>
<li><strong>特征点节点</strong>：结构的关键特征点（如载荷点、支撑点、应力集中点）作为图中的节点，适用于关键区域优化</li>
<li><strong>混合节点</strong>：结合上述多种节点定义策略，构建多层次图结构</li>
</ol>
<p>本研究主要采用单元中心节点策略，即将每个有限元单元映射为图中的一个节点。对于二维结构，节点的位置坐标为单元中心点坐标；对于三维结构，节点的位置坐标为单元的质心坐标。</p>
<h3 id="边连接建立策略">3.2.2 边连接建立策略</h3>
<p>边连接定义了节点之间的关系，对于捕获结构的拓扑特征至关重要。常见的边连接建立策略包括：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>相邻连接</strong>：如果两个单元共享边（2D）或面（3D），则在对应节点之间建立边连接</li>
<li><strong>距离阈值连接</strong>：如果两个节点之间的距离小于预设阈值，则建立边连接</li>
<li><strong>K近邻连接</strong>：每个节点与其K个最近的节点建立边连接</li>
<li><strong>物理关系连接</strong>：基于力传递路径、应力分布等物理关系建立边连接</li>
</ol>
<p>本研究主要采用相邻连接与K近邻连接相结合的策略，既考虑了局部拓扑关系，又兼顾了更广范围的结构信息传递。具体而言，对于每个节点，首先与其直接相邻的节点建立边连接，然后再与非相邻但距离最近的K个节点建立长程边连接。</p>
<p>边连接可以是有向的或无向的，取决于信息传递的需求。在本研究中主要采用无向图表示，即如果节点i与节点j之间存在连接，则信息可以双向流动。</p>
<h3 id="节点和边特征赋值">3.2.3 节点和边特征赋值</h3>
<p>节点和边特征是图神经网络学习的基础，合理的特征设计对模型性能至关重要。</p>
<p><strong>节点特征</strong>可以包括：</p>
<ul>
<li>空间位置坐标 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(x, y, z)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>材料密度 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>ρ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>材料属性（如杨氏模量、泊松比）</li>
<li>局部应力/应变状态</li>
<li>位移信息</li>
<li>单元形状特征（如面积、体积、长宽比）</li>
<li>边界条件标记（如固定、载荷、自由）</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>边特征</strong>可以包括：</p>
<ul>
<li>连接距离（节点间的欧氏距离）</li>
<li>连接方向（单位向量）</li>
<li>连接强度（可基于共享边/面的长度/面积）</li>
<li>相对位置关系（如角度、方向余弦）</li>
<li>力传递系数（基于结构分析结果）</li>
</ul>
<p>在初始阶段，节点特征主要包括位置坐标和初始密度，边特征主要包括连接距离和方向。随着优化过程的进行，可以动态更新节点和边特征，加入更多的结构响应信息。</p>
<h3 id="图构建算法">3.2.4 图构建算法</h3>
<p>基于上述策略，提出一种从有限元网格到结构图的转换算法：</p>
<pre><code>算法 3.1: 结构图构建算法
输入: 有限元网格 M，K近邻参数 K
输出: 结构图 G = (V, E)

1. 初始化节点集 V = ∅, 边集 E = ∅
2. 对于网格 M 中的每个单元 e:
   a. 计算单元中心坐标 (x_e, y_e, z_e)
   b. 创建节点 v_e，初始化节点特征 (位置、密度等)
   c. 将 v_e 添加到节点集 V
3. 对于每个节点 v_i ∈ V:
   a. 找出与 v_i 对应单元相邻的所有单元，获取对应节点集 N_adj(v_i)
   b. 对于每个节点 v_j ∈ N_adj(v_i):
      i. 计算边特征 (距离、方向等)
      ii. 创建边 (v_i, v_j) 并添加到边集 E
   c. 在剩余节点中找出距离 v_i 最近的 K 个节点，获取节点集 N_K(v_i)
   d. 对于每个节点 v_j ∈ N_K(v_i) 且 v_j ∉ N_adj(v_i):
      i. 计算边特征 (距离、方向等)
      ii. 创建边 (v_i, v_j) 并添加到边集 E
4. 返回结构图 G = (V, E)
</code></pre>
<p>该算法的时间复杂度主要由K近邻搜索决定，对于包含n个节点的图，时间复杂度为O(n²)。对于大规模结构，可以采用空间分区、KD树等技术优化K近邻搜索，将复杂度降低到O(n log n)。</p>
<h2 id="多尺度结构的图分层建模方法">3.3 多尺度结构的图分层建模方法</h2>
<p>多尺度结构优化需要同时考虑不同尺度上的结构特征和性能需求。本节提出一种图分层建模方法，通过构建层次化的图结构，实现多尺度信息的有效表示和融合。</p>
<h3 id="层次化图结构设计">3.3.1 层次化图结构设计</h3>
<p>层次化图结构包括多个层次的子图，每个层次对应不同的空间尺度。一般而言，可以构建三个主要层次：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>微观层次图</strong> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G_{\text{micro}} = (V_{\text{micro}}, E_{\text{micro}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">micro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.22222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">micro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">micro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>：表示材料微结构和细节特征</li>
<li><strong>中观层次图</strong> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G_{\text{meso}} = (V_{\text{meso}}, E_{\text{meso}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; <li><strong>宏观层次图</strong> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G_{\text{macro}} = (V_{\text{macro}}, E_{\text{macro}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; </ol>
<p>不同层次的图通过特殊的跨层边 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>cross</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">E_{\text{cross}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">cross</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 连接，形成完整的多尺度图结构：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>multi</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub><mo>∪</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub><mo>∪</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub><mo>∪</mo><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub><mo>∪</mo><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub><mo>∪</mo><msub><mi>E</mi><mtext>cross</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G_{\text{multi}} = (V_{\text{micro}} \cup V_{\text{meso}} \cup V_{\text{macro}}, E_{\text{micro}} \cup E_{\text{meso}} \cup E_{\text{macro}} \cup E_{\text{cross}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">meso</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">macro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">cross</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3 id="图粗化与细化">3.3.2 图粗化与细化</h3>
<p>图粗化（Graph Coarsening）和图细化（Graph Refinement）是构建多尺度图结构的关键操作。</p>
<p><strong>图粗化</strong>是从细尺度图生成粗尺度图的过程，主要步骤包括：</p>
<ol>
<li>节点聚类：将细尺度图中的节点分组聚类</li>
<li>超节点生成：每个聚类生成一个粗尺度图中的超节点</li>
<li>超边建立：根据聚类间的连接关系建立超边</li>
<li>特征聚合：将聚类内节点的特征聚合为超节点的特征</li>
</ol>
<p>常用的图粗化算法包括多层图划分、谱聚类、重叠社区检测等。本研究采用基于结构相似性的层次聚类方法，将具有相似材料属性和力学行为的节点聚合为超节点。</p>
<p><strong>图细化</strong>是从粗尺度图生成细尺度图的过程，主要用于局部细节优化和结果解释。图细化可以通过以下方式实现：</p>
<ol>
<li>超节点分解：将粗尺度图中的超节点分解为多个细尺度节点</li>
<li>局部结构重建：根据预定义的模板或规则重建局部细节结构</li>
<li>特征分配：将超节点的特征分配或映射到细尺度节点</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="跨尺度信息传递机制">3.3.3 跨尺度信息传递机制</h3>
<p>跨尺度信息传递是多尺度图模型的核心，它实现了不同尺度间的信息交换和协同优化。主要的信息传递机制包括：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>自顶向下传递</strong>（Top-down）：从宏观尺度向微观尺度传递全局约束和优化目标<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mtext>micro</mtext><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mtext>down</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mtext>micro</mtext><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mtext>macro</mtext><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_{\text{micro}}^{(l+1)} = f_{\text{down}}(h_{\text{micro}}^{(l)}, h_{\text{macro}}^{(l)})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.3275em; vertical-align: -0.282702em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.4173em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">micro</span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; vertical-align: -0.282702em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.282702em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">macro</span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>自底向上传递</strong>（Bottom-up）：从微观尺度向宏观尺度传递局部响应和性能指标<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mtext>macro</mtext><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mtext>up</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mtext>macro</mtext><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mtext>micro</mtext><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_{\text{macro}}^{(l+1)} = f_{\text{up}}(h_{\text{macro}}^{(l)}, h_{\text{micro}}^{(l)})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.185em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.282702em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>同层传递</strong>（Intra-level）：同一尺度内的信息传递，遵循标准GNN的消息传递机制<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mi>i</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mtext>intra</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mi>i</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mi>j</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>:</mo><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="script">N</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_{i}^{(l+1)} = f_{\text{intra}}(h_{i}^{(l)}, \{h_{j}^{(l)} : j \in \mathcal{N}(i)\})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.32166em; vertical-align: -0.276864em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42314em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; vertical-align: -0.412972em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em;
