margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.891331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">s_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是当前状态（结构图），<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是当前动作（结构修改），<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r_i(s_t, a_t)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> 是第 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65952em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span></span> 个目标对应的奖励。</p>
<h3 id="多尺度目标函数整合">3.4.3 多尺度目标函数整合</h3>
<p>多尺度优化需要整合不同尺度上的目标函数。这里使用一种层次化目标函数框架：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mtext>multi</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>multi</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>α</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>β</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>γ</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{\text{multi}}(G_{\text{multi}}) = \alpha \cdot F_{\text{macro}}(G_{\text{macro}}) + \beta \cdot F_{\text{meso}}(G_{\text{meso}}) + \gamma \cdot F_{\text{micro}}(G_{\text{micro}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">multi</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">multi</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.44445em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">macro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">macro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">meso</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">meso</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.63889em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05556em;">γ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">micro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">micro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mtext>macro</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{\text{macro}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">macro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>、<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mtext>meso</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{\text{meso}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">meso</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mtext>micro</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{\text{micro}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">micro</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 分别是宏观、中观和微观尺度的目标函数，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span></span>、<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>γ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\gamma</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05556em;">γ</span></span></span></span></span> 是权重系数，满足 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>β</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>γ</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha + \beta + \gamma = 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05556em;">γ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>。</p>
<p>在优化过程中，可以根据当前优化阶段和结构特点动态调整权重系数，实现不同尺度的协同优化。</p>
<h2 id="多目标约束下的拓扑优化建模">3.5 多目标约束下的拓扑优化建模</h2>
<p>多目标约束下的拓扑优化需要同时考虑多个性能目标和约束条件，是一类复杂的优化问题。本节讨论如何在图表示框架下建立多目标约束拓扑优化模型。</p>
<h3 id="约束条件表示">3.5.1 约束条件表示</h3>
<p>在图表示框架下，约束条件可以分为以下几类：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>全局约束</strong>：作用于整个结构的约束，如总体积约束、总重量约束<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mtext>global</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_{\text{global}}(G) \leq 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">global</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>局部约束</strong>：作用于局部区域或特定节点的约束，如局部应力约束、局部位移约束<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>local</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>i</mi><mo>∈</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mtext>local</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_{\text{local},i}(G) \leq 0, \quad i \in I_{\text{local}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">local</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.85396em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.07847em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">local</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>制造约束</strong>：考虑制造工艺的约束，如最小特征尺寸、对称性、连通性等<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>manuf</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mtext>manuf</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_{\text{manuf},j}(G) \leq 0, \quad j \in I_{\text{manuf}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">manuf</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.85396em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; </li>
<li>
<p><strong>多物理场约束</strong>：考虑多物理场耦合效应的约束，如热-力耦合、流-固耦合等<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>multi</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>k</mi><mo>∈</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mtext>multi</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_{\text{multi},k}(G) \leq 0, \quad k \in I_{\text{multi}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; </li>
</ol>
<h3 id="基于图的多目标约束优化模型">3.5.2 基于图的多目标约束优化模型</h3>
<p>基于图表示的多目标约束拓扑优化模型可以表述为：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><munder><mrow><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mi>G</mi></munder><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>F</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msup><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mi>T</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mtext>s.t.</mtext><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mtext>global</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>local</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>i</mi><mo>∈</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mtext>local</mtext></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>manuf</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mtext>manuf</mtext></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>multi</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>k</mi><mo>∈</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mtext>multi</mtext></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="script">G</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\min_{G} \quad &amp; F(G) = [f_1(G), f_2(G), \ldots, f_m(G)]^T \\
\text{s.t.} \quad &amp; g_{\text{global}}(G) \leq 0 \\
&amp; g_{\text{local},i}(G) \leq 0, \quad i \in I_{\text{local}} \\
&amp; g_{\text{manuf},j}(G) \leq 0, \quad j \in I_{\text{manuf}} \\
&amp; g_{\text{multi},k}(G) \leq 0, \quad k \in I_{\text{multi}} \\
&amp; G \in \mathcal{G}
\end{aligned}

style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.07847em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">multi</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: 0.807831em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.0593em;">G</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.46783em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{G}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.78055em; vertical-align: -0.09722em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.0593em;">G</span></span></span></span></span> 是可行图结构的集合，包含了图的拓扑约束和节点/边特征的取值范围。</p>
<h3 id="约束处理方法">3.5.3 约束处理方法</h3>
<p>在基于GNN与MORL的优化框架中，约束处理是一个关键问题。常见的约束处理方法包括：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>惩罚函数法</strong>：将约束违反程度作为惩罚项加入目标函数<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mtext>penalized</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>f</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><munder><mo>∑</mo><mi>j</mi></munder><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f_{\text{penalized}}(G) = f(G) + \sum_{j} \lambda_j \max(0, g_j(G))^2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">penalized</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.46378em; vertical-align: -1.41378em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.05001em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.87233em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.41378em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop">max</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.864108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>j</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda_j</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.980548em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是惩罚系数。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>拉格朗日乘子法</strong>：构建拉格朗日函数，同时优化原问题变量和拉格朗日乘子<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>λ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>f</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><munder><mo>∑</mo><mi>j</mi></munder><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}(G, \lambda) = f(G) + \sum_{j} \lambda_j g_j(G)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.46378em; vertical-align: -1.41378em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.05001em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.87233em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.41378em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>投影法</strong>：在每次迭代后将解投影到可行域<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>G</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mtext>Proj</mtext><mi mathvariant="script">G</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>α</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∇</mi><mi>f</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G_{t+1} = \text{Proj}_{\mathcal{G}}(G_t - \alpha \nabla f(G_t))</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.891661em; vertical-align: -0.208331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.208331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06219em; vertical-align: -0.312194em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Proj</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.234191em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.45586em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0593em;">G</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.312194em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mord">∇</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">))</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>约束奖励塑造</strong>：在MORL框架中，将约束满足程度转化为奖励信号<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mtext>constraint</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><munder><mo>∑</mo><mi>j</mi></munder><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r_{\text{constraint}}(s_t, a_t) = -\sum_{j} \max(0, g_j(G_{t+1}))^2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">constraint</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.46378em; vertical-align: -1.41378em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.05001em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.87233em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.41378em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop">max</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.208331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.864108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>在本研究中主要采用约束奖励塑造方法，将约束条件融入MORL的奖励函数设计中，引导智能体学习满足约束的优化策略。</p>
<h2 id="本章小结-1">3.6 本章小结</h2>
<p>本章提出了一种基于图表示的拓扑优化问题建模方法，包括从网格到图的转换策略、多尺度结构的图分层建模方法、性能指标定义与目标函数构造，以及多目标约束下的优化模型建立。</p>
<p>首先，我们介绍了机械结构建模的基本方法，对比了传统有限元建模和基于图的结构建模的异同。基于图的建模方法能够自然表达结构的拓扑关系，具有多尺度表示能力和高计算效率，为后续的GNN特征提取和MORL优化决策提供了基础。</p>
<p>其次，我们详细讨论了从有限元网格到图结构的转换策略，包括节点定义、边连接建立和特征赋值。提出的结构图构建算法能够有效捕获机械结构的几何和拓扑特征，为GNN模型提供高质量的输入数据。</p>
<p>然后，我们提出了一种多尺度结构的图分层建模方法，通过构建层次化的图结构，实现多尺度信息的有效表示和融合。图粗化与细化操作以及跨尺度信息传递机制是多尺度图模型的核心，能够平衡计算效率和模型表达能力。</p>
<p>接着，我们讨论了基于图表示的性能指标定义和目标函数构造方法，将传统拓扑优化中的性能指标（如柔顺度、重量、应力等）重新定义为节点级、边级和图级指标。多目标函数的构造和多尺度目标函数的整合为后续的MORL优化提供了理论基础。</p>
<p>最后，我们建立了多目标约束下的拓扑优化模型，讨论了约束条件的表示和处理方法。基于约束奖励塑造的方法将约束条件融入MORL的奖励函数设计中，为满足复杂约束的优化提供了新思路。</p>
<p>本章提出的基于图表示的拓扑优化问题建模方法，为下一章基于GNN与MORL的拓扑优化算法设计奠定了基础。通过将机械结构表示为图数据，我们能够充分发挥GNN在非欧几里得数据处理方面的优势，实现结构特征的有效提取和表示。同时，基于图的性能指标定义和目标函数构造，为MORL在多目标优化中的应用提供了必要的理论支撑。</p>
<h1 id="第四章-基于gnn与morl的拓扑优化算法设计">第四章 基于GNN与MORL的拓扑优化算法设计</h1>
<h2 id="系统框架总体架构设计">4.1 系统框架总体架构设计</h2>
<p>本章提出一种基于图神经网络(GNN)与多目标强化学习(MORL)的拓扑优化算法框架，旨在解决传统拓扑优化方法在处理多目标、多尺度问题时面临的计算效率低、搜索空间受限、难以全局最优等问题。该框架通过GNN的结构感知能力与MORL的策略学习能力相结合，实现机械结构的智能化优化设计。</p>
<h3 id="系统总体架构">4.1.1 系统总体架构</h3>
<p>基于GNN与MORL的拓扑优化系统总体架构如图4.1所示，主要包括四个核心模块：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>结构图表示模块</strong>：负责将机械结构转换为图表示，包括图构建、特征提取和多尺度表示</li>
<li><strong>GNN特征学习模块</strong>：基于图神经网络提取结构特征，捕获拓扑关系和几何信息</li>
<li><strong>MORL策略优化模块</strong>：基于多目标强化学习进行优化决策，平衡多个性能目标</li>
<li><strong>结构评估与更新模块</strong>：评估优化结果，更新结构设计，并提供反馈信息</li>
</ol>
<p>这四个模块形成一个闭环优化系统，通过迭代优化不断提升结构性能。系统的工作流程如下：</p>
<ol>
<li>输入初始结构设计和优化目标</li>
<li>将结构转换为图表示</li>
<li>通过GNN提取结构特征</li>
<li>基于MORL生成优化决策</li>
<li>更新结构设计并评估性能</li>
<li>重复步骤2-5直至满足终止条件</li>
<li>输出最终优化结构</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="系统关键特性">4.1.2 系统关键特性</h3>
<p>本系统具有以下关键特性：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>端到端学习</strong>：从结构表示到优化决策的全过程通过深度学习实现，减少人工干预</li>
<li><strong>多目标协同优化</strong>：同时考虑多个性能目标，如刚度、重量、热性能等</li>
<li><strong>多尺度结构处理</strong>：通过层次化图表示处理不同尺度的结构特征</li>
<li><strong>自适应优化策略</strong>：根据优化过程动态调整策略，避免陷入局部最优</li>
<li><strong>知识迁移能力</strong>：通过预训练模型实现知识在不同结构优化问题间的迁移</li>
<li><strong>可解释性设计</strong>：提供优化决策的解释和可视化，增强用户信任</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="系统实现架构">4.1.3 系统实现架构</h3>
<p>从实现角度，系统架构可分为以下几层：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>数据层</strong>：包括结构几何数据、材料属性数据、边界条件数据等</li>
<li><strong>表示层</strong>：实现结构到图的转换，包括节点定义、边连接、特征赋值等</li>
<li><strong>模型层</strong>：包含GNN模型和MORL模型的定义、训练和推理</li>
<li><strong>优化层</strong>：实现优化算法、约束处理和终止条件判断</li>
<li><strong>评估层</strong>：计算性能指标、生成评估报告和可视化结果</li>
<li><strong>接口层</strong>：提供与CAD/CAE系统的数据交换接口</li>
</ol>
<p>系统的软件实现采用模块化设计，各模块之间通过标准化接口进行数据交换，便于扩展和维护。核心算法使用Python实现，结合PyTorch等深度学习框架和NetworkX等图处理库。</p>
<h2 id="gnn特征提取模型设计与训练">4.2 GNN特征提取模型设计与训练</h2>
<p>GNN特征提取模型是系统的核心组件之一，负责从结构图表示中提取有意义的特征，为后续的优化决策提供依据。本节详细介绍GNN模型的设计与训练方法。</p>
<h3 id="结构感知特征学习">4.2.1 结构感知特征学习</h3>
<h5 id="图神经网络架构设计">图神经网络架构设计</h5>
<p>本研究设计了一种多层次的图神经网络架构，能够有效捕获机械结构的拓扑特征和几何信息。该架构包括以下关键组件：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>图卷积层</strong>：使用图卷积网络(GCN)进行局部特征聚合<br>

vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.92019em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.60233em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.19444em;"><span class="mord">~</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是对应的度矩阵，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>H</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H^{(l)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.888em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是第 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>l</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">l</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span></span> 层的节点特征矩阵，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>W</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W^{(l)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.888em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">W</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是可学习的权重矩阵，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>σ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">σ</span></span></span></span></span> 是非线性激活函数。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>图注意力层</strong>：使用图注意力网络(GAT)学习节点间的重要性权重<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mi>i</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mi>σ</mi><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><munder><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="script">N</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>∪</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow></munder><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mi>j</mi></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><msup><mi>W</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mi>j</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_i^{(l+1)} = \sigma\left(\sum_{j \in \mathcal{N}(i) \cup \{i\}} \alpha_{ij}^{(l)} W^{(l)} h_j^{(l)}\right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.32166em; vertical-align: -0.276864em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42314em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.276864em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.60004em; vertical-align: -1.55002em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">σ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen"><span class="delimsizing mult"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.05002em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.25em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.155em;"></span><span class="delimsizinginner delim-size4"><span class="">⎝</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.397em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.155em;"></span><span class="" style="height: 0.016em; 其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>α</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mi>j</mi></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha_{ij}^{(l)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.45777em; vertical-align: -0.412972em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42314em; margin-left: -0.0037em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">ij</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.2198em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span></span> 对节点 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65952em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span></span> 的重要性。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>跳跃连接</strong>：引入残差连接，缓解深层网络的梯度消失问题<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>H</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>H</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mtext>GNN</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>H</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H^{(l+1)} = H^{(l)} + \text{GNN}(H^{(l)})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.938em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.02133em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em;
