vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">GNN</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>多尺度特征融合</strong>：整合不同感受野的特征，捕获多尺度结构信息<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>H</mi><mtext>multi</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mtext>Concat</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>H</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>H</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>H</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>L</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msub><mi>W</mi><mtext>fusion</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H_{\text{multi}} = \text{Concat}(H^{(1)}, H^{(2)}, ..., H^{(L)})W_{\text{fusion}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.08125em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">multi</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Concat</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight">2</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">...</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">W</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">fusion</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>全局池化</strong>：将节点级特征聚合为图级特征<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mi>G</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mtext>Readout</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi>v</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>∈</mo><mi>V</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_G = \text{Readout}(\{h_i | v_i \in V\})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">G</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Readout</span></span><span class="mopen">({</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">})</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中，Readout可以是平均池化、最大池化或注意力池化等。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>完整的GNN特征提取模型可以表示为以下伪代码：</p>
<pre><code>算法 4.1: GNN特征提取模型
输入: 结构图 G = (V, E)，节点特征 X，边特征 E_feat
输出: 节点级特征 H_node，图级特征 h_graph

1. 初始化 H^(0) = X
2. 对于 l = 0 到 L-1:
   a. 消息传递: M^(l) = Message(H^(l), E_feat)
   b. 消息聚合: A^(l) = Aggregate(M^(l))
   c. 节点更新: H^(l+1) = Update(H^(l), A^(l))
   d. 如果使用跳跃连接: H^(l+1) = H^(l) + H^(l+1)
3. 多尺度特征融合: H_node = Fusion(H^(0), H^(1), ..., H^(L))
4. 图池化: h_graph = Readout(H_node)
5. 返回 H_node, h_graph
</code></pre>
<h5 id="特征表示学习">特征表示学习</h5>
<p>为了有效表示机械结构的特性，GNN模型需要学习以下几类特征：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>局部拓扑特征</strong>：捕获节点的局部连接模式和邻域结构</li>
<li><strong>全局结构特征</strong>：理解整体结构布局和主要受力路径</li>
<li><strong>物理属性特征</strong>：编码材料属性、应力分布等物理信息</li>
<li><strong>边界条件特征</strong>：表示载荷、约束等边界条件信息</li>
</ol>
<p>特征学习采用多任务学习框架，同时优化多个相关任务，提高特征的泛化能力：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>total</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>reconstruction</mtext></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>property</mtext></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>clustering</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{total}} = \lambda_1 \mathcal{L}_{\text{reconstruction}} + \lambda_2 \mathcal{L}_{\text{property}} + \lambda_3 \mathcal{L}_{\text{clustering}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">reconstruction</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.980548em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">property</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.980548em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">clustering</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>reconstruction</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{reconstruction}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">reconstruction</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是结构重建损失，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>property</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{property}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">property</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是物理属性预测损失，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>clustering</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{clustering}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">clustering</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是结构聚类损失，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda_1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>、<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda_2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 和 <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda_3</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是权重系数。</p>
<h3 id="动态图更新机制">4.2.2 动态图更新机制</h3>
<p>在拓扑优化过程中，结构不断演化，图表示也需要相应更新。本研究设计了一种动态图更新机制，能够高效处理结构变化。</p>
<h5 id="增量图更新算法">增量图更新算法</h5>
<p>增量图更新算法避免了每次优化迭代都重新构建完整图的计算开销，只更新发生变化的部分：</p>
<pre><code>算法 4.2: 增量图更新算法
输入: 当前图 G_t = (V_t, E_t)，结构变化 Δ
输出: 更新后的图 G_{t+1} = (V_{t+1}, E_{t+1})

1. 初始化 V_{t+1} = V_t, E_{t+1} = E_t
2. 对于每个添加的节点 v_new:
   a. 将 v_new 添加到 V_{t+1}
   b. 初始化 v_new 的特征
   c. 找出与 v_new 相邻的节点集合 N(v_new)
   d. 对于每个节点 u ∈ N(v_new):
      i. 创建边 (v_new, u) 并添加到 E_{t+1}
      ii. 计算边特征
3. 对于每个删除的节点 v_del:
   a. 从 V_{t+1} 中移除 v_del
   b. 从 E_{t+1} 中移除所有与 v_del 相连的边
4. 对于每个修改的节点 v_mod:
   a. 更新 v_mod 的节点特征
   b. 更新与 v_mod 相连的边的特征
5. 返回 G_{t+1} = (V_{t+1}, E_{t+1})
</code></pre>
<h5 id="特征传递与记忆机制">特征传递与记忆机制</h5>
<p>为了保持优化过程中的信息连续性，设计了特征传递与记忆机制：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>短期记忆</strong>：保存最近几次迭代的图表示和特征，用于计算变化趋势<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>H</mi><mtext>short</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi>H</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>H</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>H</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H_{\text{short}} = [H_{t-k}, H_{t-k+1}, ..., H_t]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.08125em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>长期记忆</strong>：使用循环神经网络(RNN)或注意力机制捕获长期演化模式<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mtext>long</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mtext>RNN</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mtext>long</mtext><mtext>prev</mtext></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h_{\text{long}} = \text{RNN}(h_{\text{long}}^{\text{prev}}, h_t)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.980548em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; vertical-align: -0.437416em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">RNN</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7823em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.39869em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">long</span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">prev</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.437416em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>特征传递</strong>：将历史信息融入当前特征更新<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>H</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mtext>GNN</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi>H</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mtext>short</mtext></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mtext>long</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H_{t+1} = \text{GNN}(X_{t+1}, [H_t, h_{\text{short}}, h_{\text{long}}])</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.891661em; vertical-align: -0.208331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.08125em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.208331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">GNN</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.07847em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.208331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.08125em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">short</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">long</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">])</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>这种记忆机制使模型能够学习结构演化的时序模式，提高优化效率。</p>
<h3 id="gnn模型训练策略">4.2.3 GNN模型训练策略</h3>
<h5 id="训练数据生成">训练数据生成</h5>
<p>GNN模型的训练需要大量高质量的数据。本研究采用以下方法生成训练数据：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>仿真数据生成</strong>：使用有限元分析(FEA)生成结构-性能对应数据</li>
<li><strong>数据增强</strong>：通过旋转、镜像、缩放等操作扩充数据集</li>
<li><strong>迁移学习数据</strong>：利用已有优化案例的数据进行迁移学习</li>
<li><strong>主动学习采样</strong>：根据模型不确定性选择最有价值的样本进行标注</li>
</ol>
<h5 id="训练算法">训练算法</h5>
<p>GNN模型的训练采用端到端的监督学习方法，结合自监督学习提高特征质量：</p>
<pre><code>算法 4.3: GNN模型训练算法
输入: 训练数据集 D = {(G_i, y_i)}_{i=1}^N，学习率 η，批次大小 B，训练轮数 E
输出: 训练好的GNN模型参数 θ

1. 初始化模型参数 θ
2. 对于 epoch = 1 到 E:
   a. 将数据集 D 随机打乱并分成大小为 B 的批次
   b. 对于每个批次 (G_batch, y_batch):
      i. 前向传播: H_node, h_graph = GNN(G_batch; θ)
      ii. 计算损失: L = Loss(H_node, h_graph, y_batch)
      iii. 反向传播: 计算梯度 ∇_θ L
      iv. 参数更新: θ = θ - η·∇_θ L
   c. 在验证集上评估模型性能
   d. 如果满足早停条件，则停止训练
3. 返回最佳模型参数 θ*
</code></pre>
<h5 id="正则化与优化技术">正则化与优化技术</h5>
<p>为提高模型泛化能力和训练稳定性，采用以下正则化与优化技术：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Dropout</strong>：在图卷积层之间添加Dropout，防止过拟合</li>
<li><strong>批归一化</strong>：加速训练收敛并提高稳定性</li>
<li><strong>权重衰减</strong>：L2正则化控制模型复杂度</li>
<li><strong>学习率调度</strong>：使用余弦退火等策略动态调整学习率</li>
<li><strong>梯度裁剪</strong>：防止梯度爆炸问题</li>
<li><strong>对比学习</strong>：通过对比正负样本对提高特征区分能力</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="morl优化策略设计">4.3 MORL优化策略设计</h2>
<p>多目标强化学习(MORL)优化策略是系统的另一核心组件，负责基于GNN提取的特征生成优化决策，平衡多个性能目标。本节详细介绍MORL模型的设计与训练方法。</p>
<h3 id="多目标奖励函数设计">4.3.1 多目标奖励函数设计</h3>
<h5 id="奖励函数构造">奖励函数构造</h5>
<p>MORL的核心是设计合适的多目标奖励函数，准确反映不同性能目标的优化程度。本研究设计的多目标奖励函数包括以下组成部分：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>刚度奖励</strong>：评估结构刚度性能<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mtext>stiffness</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mtext>ref</mtext></msub></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r_{\text{stiffness}}(s_t, a_t) = -\frac{c(s_{t+1})}{c_{\text{ref}}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">stiffness</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.263em; vertical-align: -0.836em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ref</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.208331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.836em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c(s_{t+1})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ref</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是参考柔顺度。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>重量奖励</strong>：评估结构轻量化程度<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mtext>weight</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>w</mi><mtext>ref</mtext></msub></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r_{\text{weight}}(s_t, a_t) = -\frac{w(s_{t+1})}{w_{\text{ref}}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; 其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>w</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">w(s_{t+1})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; </li>
<li>
<p><strong>应力奖励</strong>：评估结构应力分布均匀性<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mtext>stress</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mtext>max</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mtext>allow</mtext></msub></mfrac><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>σ</mi></msub><mo>⋅</mo><mtext>Var</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>σ</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r_{\text{stress}}(s_t, a_t) = -\frac{\sigma_{\text{max}}(s_{t+1})}{\sigma_{\text{allow}}} - \lambda_{\sigma} \cdot \text{Var}(\sigma(s_{t+1}))</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; 其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mtext>max</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma_{\text{max}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">max</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是最大应力，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mtext>allow</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma_{\text{allow}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">allow</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是允许应力，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Var</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>σ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Var}(\sigma)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Var</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">σ</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> 是应力方差。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>制造性奖励</strong>：评估结构的可制造性<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mtext>manuf</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><munder><mo>∑</mo><mi>i</mi></munder><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>manuf</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r_{\text{manuf}}(s_t, a_t) = -\sum_{i} \max(0, g_{\text{manuf},i}(s_{t+1}))^2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">manuf</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.32767em; vertical-align: -1.27767em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.05001em;"><span class="" style="top: -1.87233em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05001em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.27767em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop">max</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">manuf</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; 其中，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mtext>manuf</mtext><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_{\text{manuf},i}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.716668em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">manuf</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 是制造约束函数。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>变化奖励</strong>：鼓励探索新的设计空间<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>r</mi><mtext>change</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>β</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mtext>Novelty</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r_{\text{change}}(s_t, a_t) = \beta \cdot \text{Novelty}(s_{t+1}, \{s_{t-k}, ..., s_t\})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">change</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Novelty</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.208331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em;
