</table><p>从消融实验结果可以得出以下结论：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>GNN组件贡献</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>注意力机制提升优化质量2.3个百分点，但增加计算时间</li>
<li>跳跃连接提升优化质量3.1个百分点，对收敛速度有显著影响</li>
<li>多尺度融合提升优化质量4.5个百分点，是GNN模型中最关键的组件</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>MORL组件贡献</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>多策略学习提升优化质量1.6个百分点</li>
<li>动态权重调整提升优化质量2.0个百分点</li>
<li>Pareto优势函数提升优化质量3.3个百分点，对多目标优化至关重要</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>融合机制贡献</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>端到端训练提升优化质量2.5个百分点，对收敛速度有显著影响</li>
<li>知识迁移提升优化质量1.7个百分点，提高了模型泛化能力</li>
<li>梯度流控制提升优化质量3.0个百分点，对训练稳定性至关重要</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p>消融实验表明，系统各组件都对整体性能有显著贡献，其中多尺度融合、Pareto优势函数和梯度流控制是最关键的组件。</p>
<h3 id="鲁棒性测试">5.7.2 鲁棒性测试</h3>
<p>为了验证算法的鲁棒性，本研究设计了以下测试：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>输入噪声测试</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>向结构几何添加不同程度的噪声(0%-10%)</li>
<li>向材料属性添加不同程度的噪声(0%-10%)</li>
<li>向边界条件添加不同程度的噪声(0%-10%)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参数扰动测试</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>对GNN模型参数进行不同程度的扰动</li>
<li>对MORL模型参数进行不同程度的扰动</li>
<li>对目标权重进行不同程度的扰动</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>网格分辨率测试</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>在不同分辨率的网格上测试算法性能</li>
<li>分辨率范围从20×20到200×200</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p>鲁棒性测试结果表明：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>输入噪声影响</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>在5%以下的几何噪声下，优化质量下降不超过2%</li>
<li>在5%以下的材料属性噪声下，优化质量下降不超过3%</li>
<li>在5%以下的边界条件噪声下，优化质量下降不超过4%</li>
<li>本文方法比传统方法对噪声更加鲁棒，特别是对几何噪声</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参数扰动影响</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>GNN参数±10%扰动导致优化质量下降约2%</li>
<li>MORL参数±10%扰动导致优化质量下降约3%</li>
<li>目标权重±20%扰动导致Pareto前沿覆盖范围变化，但质量保持稳定</li>
<li>端到端训练的模型比分别训练的模型对参数扰动更加鲁棒</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>网格分辨率影响</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>本文方法在不同分辨率下表现稳定，优化质量变化不超过5%</li>
<li>传统方法在高分辨率下计算时间急剧增加，而本文方法增加较缓慢</li>
<li>本文方法在低分辨率下也能获得较好结果，适合快速概念设计</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p>综合鲁棒性测试结果表明，本文提出的方法具有良好的鲁棒性，能够在各种扰动和变化条件下保持稳定的优化性能，这对于实际工程应用至关重要。</p>
<h2 id="本章小结-3">5.8 本章小结</h2>
<p>本章通过一系列实验对基于GNN与MORL的拓扑优化算法进行了全面评估。主要结论如下：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>不同GNN模型对拓扑优化性能有显著影响，本文提出的混合GNN模型在特征提取能力和计算效率之间取得了最佳平衡，优化质量达到96.3%。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>多目标函数配置对优化结果有重要影响，MORL框架能够有效平衡多个性能目标，生成均匀分布的Pareto最优解集。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>多尺度协同优化方法在处理晶格结构、复合材料和功能梯度材料等多尺度问题时表现出色，综合性能比单尺度优化提高约27%。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>与传统方法和其他机器学习方法相比，本文方法在优化质量、收敛速度、计算效率、多目标处理和多尺度处理等方面均具有显著优势。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>消融实验表明系统各组件都对整体性能有重要贡献，其中多尺度融合、Pareto优势函数和梯度流控制是最关键的组件。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>鲁棒性测试表明本文方法对输入噪声、参数扰动和网格分辨率变化具有良好的适应性，能够在各种条件下保持稳定的优化性能。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>实验结果充分验证了本文提出的基于GNN与MORL的拓扑优化方法的有效性和优越性，为机械结构的智能化优化设计提供了新的解决方案。该方法在处理复杂的多目标、多尺度拓扑优化问题时具有显著优势，有望在航空航天、汽车工业、医疗器械等领域得到广泛应用。</p>
<h1 id="第六章-结论与展望">第六章 结论与展望</h1>
<h2 id="研究成果总结">6.1 研究成果总结</h2>
<p>本文提出了一种基于图神经网络(GNN)与多目标强化学习(MORL)的机械结构多尺度拓扑优化方法，旨在解决传统拓扑优化方法在处理多目标、多尺度问题时面临的计算效率低、搜索空间受限、难以全局最优等问题。通过系统研究和实验验证，本文取得了以下主要研究成果：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>提出了基于图表示的机械结构建模方法</strong></p>
<p>本文提出了一种从有限元网格到图结构的转换策略，包括节点定义、边连接建立和特征赋值。这种表示方法能够自然捕获结构的拓扑关系，为后续的GNN特征提取提供了基础。同时，设计了多尺度结构的图分层建模方法，通过层次化图结构和跨尺度信息传递机制，实现了多尺度信息的有效表示和融合。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>设计了结构感知的GNN特征提取模型</strong></p>
<p>本文设计了一种多层次的图神经网络架构，结合GCN、GAT和跳跃连接等技术，能够有效捕获机械结构的拓扑特征和几何信息。同时，提出了动态图更新机制，通过增量图更新算法和特征传递与记忆机制，高效处理优化过程中的结构变化。实验表明，所设计的混合GNN模型在特征提取能力和计算效率之间取得了最佳平衡。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>构建了基于MORL的多目标优化策略</strong></p>
<p>本文构建了基于Actor-Critic框架的MORL网络架构，设计了多目标奖励函数和协同训练算法，实现了多个性能目标的平衡优化。通过动态权重调整、Pareto前沿探索和多策略学习等技术，系统能够在单次运行中生成多样化的Pareto最优解，为设计者提供丰富的选择。实验表明，所提出的MORL策略能够有效处理目标间的冲突和权衡。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>实现了GNN与MORL的有效融合</strong></p>
<p>本文提出了一种端到端的GNN-MORL融合架构，设计了前向信息流、反向信息流和横向信息流，实现了结构表示与优化决策的无缝连接。通过预训练与微调相结合的联合训练策略和梯度流控制机制，系统能够稳定高效地学习优化策略。同时，设计了知识迁移与泛化机制，提高了模型在新问题上的适应能力。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>建立了完整的实验评估体系</strong></p>
<p>本文构建了包含基准测试、多目标优化和多尺度结构的综合数据集，设计了全面的实验方案，从优化质量、收敛速度、计算效率、多目标处理和多尺度处理等多个维度评估算法性能。实验结果表明，所提出的方法在各项指标上均优于传统方法和其他机器学习方法，特别是在处理复杂的多目标、多尺度问题时具有显著优势。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>通过上述研究成果，本文构建了一个集建模、特征提取、优化控制于一体的智能拓扑优化系统，为机械结构的智能化设计提供了新的方法和工具。该系统能够高效处理复杂的多目标、多尺度拓扑优化问题，生成高质量的优化结构，为工程实践提供有力支持。</p>
<h2 id="创新点回顾">6.2 创新点回顾</h2>
<p>本文的主要创新点包括：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>面向机械结构的图建模策略</strong></p>
<p>传统的拓扑优化方法通常基于像素/体素表示结构，难以有效捕获拓扑关系。本文提出的图建模策略将机械结构表示为节点和边的集合，自然保留了结构的拓扑信息。创新点在于：</p>
<ul>
<li>设计了从有限元网格到图结构的系统转换方法</li>
<li>提出了节点特征和边特征的构造策略，编码结构的几何和物理信息</li>
<li>开发了适应不同类型结构的图构建算法，提高了表示的通用性</li>
</ul>
<p>这种基于图的表示方法为后续的深度学习处理提供了理想的数据结构，克服了传统表示方法的局限性。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>GNN与MORL在结构拓扑优化中的融合</strong></p>
<p>本文首次实现了GNN与MORL在结构拓扑优化中的有机融合，构建了端到端的优化框架。创新点在于：</p>
<ul>
<li>设计了GNN特征提取与MORL决策的接口机制，实现信息的无缝流动</li>
<li>提出了联合训练策略，通过梯度流控制保证训练稳定性</li>
<li>开发了知识迁移机制，提高模型在新问题上的泛化能力</li>
</ul>
<p>这种融合充分发挥了GNN的结构感知能力和MORL的多目标决策能力，形成了互补优势，提高了整体系统性能。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>多尺度联合优化机制</strong></p>
<p>传统的多尺度优化通常采用分层策略，难以捕获尺度间的耦合效应。本文提出的多尺度联合优化机制能够同时考虑不同尺度的结构特征和性能需求。创新点在于：</p>
<ul>
<li>设计了层次化图结构，表示不同尺度的结构信息</li>
<li>提出了跨尺度信息传递机制，实现尺度间的协同优化</li>
<li>开发了多尺度目标函数整合方法，平衡不同尺度的优化目标</li>
</ul>
<p>实验表明，多尺度联合优化机制能够显著提高综合性能，特别是对于晶格结构、复合材料和功能梯度材料等多尺度结构。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>多目标强化学习激励函数设计方法</strong></p>
<p>多目标优化中的奖励设计是关键挑战之一。本文提出的多目标强化学习激励函数设计方法能够有效指导优化过程。创新点在于：</p>
<ul>
<li>设计了多维奖励向量，分别对应不同性能目标</li>
<li>提出了奖励归一化与平衡策略，处理不同目标的量纲和重要性差异</li>
<li>开发了基于Pareto支配关系的优势函数，提高多目标探索效率</li>
</ul>
<p>这种奖励函数设计方法提高了优化效率和收敛稳定性，能够生成高质量的Pareto最优解集。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>结构优化的端到端学习框架</strong></p>
<p>传统的优化方法通常需要大量人工干预和参数调整。本文提出的端到端学习框架能够自动完成从结构表示到优化决策的全过程。创新点在于：</p>
<ul>
<li>实现了从结构图到优化决策的端到端映射</li>
<li>设计了自适应优化策略，根据优化进程动态调整</li>
<li>提供了优化决策的解释和可视化，增强用户信任</li>
</ul>
<p>这种端到端框架减少了人工干预，提高了优化效率，为结构设计的智能化提供了新思路。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>这些创新点相互关联、相互支撑，共同构成了本文的理论体系和技术框架，为机械结构拓扑优化领域带来了新的方法和视角。</p>
<h2 id="存在的不足">6.3 存在的不足</h2>
<p>尽管本文提出的方法在多个方面表现出优越性，但仍存在以下不足和局限性：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>计算复杂度挑战</strong></p>
<p>虽然相比传统方法有所改进，但对于超大规模结构（如百万级网格），系统的计算复杂度仍然较高。特别是在多尺度优化中，需要同时处理不同尺度的图表示，内存占用较大。未来需要进一步优化算法，提高大规模问题的处理能力。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>物理约束的精确满足</strong></p>
<p>当前方法主要通过奖励函数引导优化过程满足物理约束，但对于严格的物理约束（如应力约束、频率约束等），可能无法保证精确满足。这可能导致在某些高精度要求的场景下，优化结果需要进一步验证和调整。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>训练数据依赖性</strong></p>
<p>作为一种基于学习的方法，系统性能在一定程度上依赖于训练数据的质量和覆盖范围。对于训练数据中未充分表示的结构类型或载荷条件，模型泛化能力可能受限。构建全面的训练数据集仍是一个挑战。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>模型可解释性有限</strong></p>
<p>尽管本文尝试提供优化决策的解释，但深度学习模型的"黑盒"特性使得完全理解决策过程仍然困难。这可能影响工程师对优化结果的信任和接受度，特别是在安全关键应用中。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>多物理场耦合处理不足</strong></p>
<p>当前方法主要关注结构力学性能，对热-力、流-固等多物理场耦合问题的处理能力有限。多物理场问题中的复杂相互作用需要更精细的建模和优化策略。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>实时优化能力不足</strong></p>
<p>虽然计算效率有所提高，但系统尚未达到实时优化的能力，难以支持交互式设计过程。设计迭代中的实时反馈对提高设计效率至关重要，这方面仍有改进空间。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>工程实现的挑战</strong></p>
<p>将本文方法集成到现有CAD/CAE系统中仍面临接口兼容性、数据交换标准等挑战。此外，工程应用中的各种制造约束和实际条件可能需要进一步的适应性调整。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>认识这些不足有助于指导未来的研究方向，推动方法的持续改进和完善。</p>
<h2 id="后续研究建议与发展展望">6.4 后续研究建议与发展展望</h2>
<p>基于本文的研究成果和存在的不足，提出以下后续研究建议和发展展望：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>高效计算策略研究</strong></p>
<p>为解决大规模问题的计算挑战，建议研究以下方向：</p>
<ul>
<li>开发图粗化和细化的自适应策略，根据优化阶段动态调整图分辨率</li>
<li>探索模型压缩和量化技术，减少内存占用和计算开销</li>
<li>研究分布式优化算法，利用并行计算加速大规模问题求解</li>
<li>开发增量更新策略，避免每次迭代重新计算整个结构</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>物理约束处理机制改进</strong></p>
<p>为提高物理约束的满足度，建议研究以下方向：</p>
<ul>
<li>开发基于拉格朗日乘子的约束处理方法，确保严格约束的精确满足</li>
<li>探索可微分物理模拟技术，将物理约束直接集成到优化流程中</li>
<li>研究混合优化策略，结合传统方法的精确性和学习方法的效率</li>
<li>设计针对特定约束类型的专用处理模块，提高约束满足的精确性</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>数据高效学习方法</strong></p>
<p>为减少对大量训练数据的依赖，建议研究以下方向：</p>
<ul>
<li>探索少样本学习和元学习技术，提高模型在有限数据下的泛化能力</li>
<li>开发主动学习策略，智能选择最有价值的样本进行标注和学习</li>
<li>研究自监督学习方法，利用未标注数据提高特征质量</li>
<li>设计数据增强技术，通过物理变换和扰动扩充训练数据集</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>可解释AI技术应用</strong></p>
<p>为提高模型可解释性，建议研究以下方向：</p>
<ul>
<li>开发基于注意力机制的可视化工具，展示决策过程中的关注区域</li>
<li>探索可解释的强化学习算法，提供决策理由和依据</li>
<li>研究神经符号结合方法，融合规则推理和深度学习的优势</li>
<li>设计交互式解释界面，允许用户查询和理解优化决策</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>多物理场优化框架</strong></p>
<p>为增强多物理场耦合问题的处理能力，建议研究以下方向：</p>
<ul>
<li>开发多物理场图表示方法，捕获不同物理场之间的相互作用</li>
<li>探索物理信息增强的图神经网络，提高物理建模能力</li>
<li>研究多任务学习框架，同时优化多个物理性能指标</li>
<li>设计针对特定多物理场问题的专用奖励函数和优化策略</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>实时优化技术</strong></p>
<p>为实现实时优化能力，建议研究以下方向：</p>
<ul>
<li>开发渐进式优化策略，快速生成粗略解并逐步精细化</li>
<li>探索神经网络加速技术，如模型蒸馏和硬件加速</li>
<li>研究增量优化方法，只更新设计变更区域的结构</li>
<li>设计交互式优化界面，支持设计师实时干预和调整</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>工程应用与系统集成</strong></p>
<p>为促进方法的工程应用，建议研究以下方向：</p>
<ul>
<li>开发与主流CAD/CAE系统的接口和插件，实现无缝集成</li>
<li>探索特定行业应用案例，如航空航天、汽车、医疗器械等</li>
<li>研究制造约束的自动识别和处理方法，提高结果可制造性</li>
<li>设计用户友好的操作界面，降低使用门槛</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>新兴技术融合</strong></p>
<p>为拓展方法的应用边界，建议探索与以下新兴技术的融合：</p>
<ul>
<li>数字孪生：将优化系统与数字孪生平台结合，实现实时优化和监控</li>
<li>增材制造：针对3D打印等新型制造工艺开发专用优化策略</li>
<li>可编程材料：将材料设计与结构优化结合，实现功能一体化设计</li>
<li>边缘计算：将优化算法部署到边缘设备，支持现场实时优化</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p>随着人工智能技术的快速发展和计算能力的持续提升，基于GNN与MORL的拓扑优化方法有望在更广泛的工程领域得到应用。未来，这种智能优化方法将与传统工程设计方法深度融合，形成新一代智能设计范式，推动机械结构设计向更加自动化、智能化和高效化方向发展。</p>
<h2 id="附录">附录</h2>
<h3 id="a.1-关键算法伪代码与实现细节">A.1 关键算法伪代码与实现细节</h3>
<p>本附录提供了论文中提出的关键算法的详细伪代码和实现细节，以便读者更深入地理解算法原理和实现方法。</p>
<h4 id="a.1.1-结构图构建算法">A.1.1 结构图构建算法</h4>
<p>结构图构建算法是将有限元网格转换为图表示的关键步骤，其详细伪代码如下：</p>
<pre><code>**算法 A.1:** 结构图构建算法
输入: 有限元网格 M，K近邻参数 K
输出: 结构图 G = (V, E)

1. 初始化节点集 V = ∅, 边集 E = ∅
2. 对于网格 M 中的每个单元 e:
   a. 计算单元中心坐标 (x_e, y_e, z_e)
   b. 初始化节点特征向量 f_e = [x_e, y_e, z_e, ρ_e, E_e, ...]
      其中 ρ_e 是单元密度，E_e 是单元杨氏模量
   c. 创建节点 v_e = (id_e, f_e)
   d. 将 v_e 添加到节点集 V
3. 构建空间索引结构 S 用于快速近邻搜索
4. 对于每个节点 v_i ∈ V:
   a. 找出与 v_i 对应单元相邻的所有单元，获取对应节点集 N_adj(v_i)
   b. 对于每个节点 v_j ∈ N_adj(v_i):
      i. 计算边特征向量 f_{ij} = [d_{ij}, θ_{ij}, w_{ij}, ...]
         其中 d_{ij} 是节点间距离，θ_{ij} 是方向角，w_{ij} 是连接强度
      ii. 创建边 e_{ij} = (v_i, v_j, f_{ij})
      iii. 将 e_{ij} 添加到边集 E
   c. 使用空间索引 S 找出距离 v_i 最近的 K 个节点，获取节点集 N_K(v_i)
   d. 对于每个节点 v_j ∈ N_K(v_i) 且 v_j ∉ N_adj(v_i):
      i. 计算边特征向量 f_{ij} = [d_{ij}, θ_{ij}, w_{ij}, ...]
      ii. 创建长程边 e_{ij} = (v_i, v_j, f_{ij})
      iii. 将 e_{ij} 添加到边集 E
5. 返回结构图 G = (V, E)
</code></pre>
<p>实现细节：</p>
<ul>
<li>空间索引结构可以使用KD树或R树实现，提高近邻搜索效率</li>
<li>边特征计算可以包含更多物理信息，如应力传递系数、热传导系数等</li>
<li>对于大规模网格，可以采用分块处理策略，减少内存占用</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="a.1.2-gnn特征提取算法">A.1.2 GNN特征提取算法</h4>
<p>GNN特征提取算法是从结构图中提取有意义特征的核心组件，其详细伪代码如下：</p>
<pre><code>**算法 A.2:** GNN特征提取算法
输入: 结构图 G = (V, E)，层数 L，隐藏维度 d
输出: 节点特征 H_node，图特征 h_graph

1. 初始化节点特征矩阵 H^(0) ∈ R^{|V|×d_in}，其中 H^(0)_i = f_i
2. 初始化边特征矩阵 E_feat ∈ R^{|E|×d_e}，其中 E_feat_{ij} = f_{ij}
3. 对于 l = 0 到 L-1:
   a. // 图卷积层
      H_GCN^(l+1) = σ(Â·H^(l)·W_GCN^(l))
      其中 Â = D^(-1/2)·(A+I)·D^(-1/2)，A 是邻接矩阵，D 是度矩阵
   
   b. // 图注意力层
      初始化 H_GAT^(l+1) = 0
      对于每个注意力头 h = 1 到 H:
         i. 计算注意力系数 α_{ij}^h = softmax_j(LeakyReLU(a^h·[W_h^(l)·h_i^(l) || W_h^(l)·h_j^(l)]))
         ii. 聚合特征 h_i^h = σ(∑_{j∈N(i)} α_{ij}^h·W_h^(l)·h_j^(l))
         iii. H_GAT^(l+1) = H_GAT^(l+1) + h_i^h / H
   
   c. // 特征融合
      H^(l+1) = β_1·H_GCN^(l+1) + β_2·H_GAT^(l+1) + β_3·H^(l)
      其中 β_1, β_2, β_3 是融合权重，满足 β_1 + β_2 + β_3 = 1
   
4. // 多尺度特征融合
   H_multi = Concat([H^(1), H^(2), ..., H^(L)])·W_fusion
   
5. // 图池化
   h_graph = 0
   对于每个节点 v_i ∈ V:
      a. 计算注意力权重 α_i = σ(w_a·tanh(W_p·h_i^(L) + b_p))
      b. h_graph = h_graph + α_i·h_i^(L)
   
6. 返回 H_node = H_multi, h_graph
</code></pre>
<p>实现细节：</p>
<ul>
<li>激活函数σ可以选择ReLU、LeakyReLU或ELU等</li>
<li>注意力机制可以使用多头注意力，提高特征提取能力</li>
<li>图池化可以使用注意力池化、平均池化或最大池化等方法</li>
<li>可以添加批归一化或层归一化，提高训练稳定性</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="a.1.3-morl优化算法">A.1.3 MORL优化算法</h4>
<p>MORL优化算法是生成多目标优化决策的核心组件，其详细伪代码如下：</p>
<pre><code>**算法 A.3:** MOPPO优化算法
输入: 初始策略参数 θ，初始价值参数 φ，学习率 η_π 和 η_Q，折扣因子 γ，
     GAE参数 λ，剪裁参数 ε，训练轮数 K，目标数量 m
输出: 训练好的策略参数 θ* 和价值参数 φ*

1. 初始化经验回放缓冲区 D
2. 对于 k = 1 到 K:
   a. 采样目标权重向量 w ~ p(w)，其中 w ∈ R^m, ∑_i w_i = 1, w_i ≥ 0
   b. 初始化轨迹 τ = {}
   c. 获取初始状态 s_0
   d. 对于 t = 0 到 T-1:
      i. 使用当前策略选择动作 a_t ~ π_θ(a|s_t, w)
      ii. 执行动作 a_t，观察奖励向量 r_t ∈ R^m 和下一状态 s_{t+1}
      iii. 将 (s_t, a_t, r_t, s_{t+1}, w) 添加到轨迹 τ
   e. 计算每个目标的折扣回报和优势函数:
      对于 i = 1 到 m:
         i. 对于 t = 0 到 T-1:
            G_t^i = ∑_{k=0}^{T-t-1} γ^k·r_{t+k}^i
            δ_t^i = r_t^i + γ·V_φ^i(s_{t+1}) - V_φ^i(s_t)
            A_t^i = ∑_{k=0}^{T-t-1} (γλ)^k·δ_{t+k}^i
   f. 计算加权优势函数:
      对于 t = 0 到 T-1:
         A_t^w = ∑_{i=1}^m w_i·A_t^i
   g. 将轨迹数据 {(s_t, a_t, r_t, s_{t+1}, A_t^1, ..., A_t^m, A_t^w, w)} 添加到回放缓冲区 D
   h. 对于每个优化迭代 j = 1 到 J:
      i. 从 D 中采样小批量数据 B
      ii. 计算策略比率 r_t(θ) = π_θ(a_t|s_t, w) / π_θ_old(a_t|s_t, w)
      iii. 计算策略损失:
           L_π(θ) = -E_B[min(r_t(θ)·A_t^w, clip(r_t(θ), 1-ε, 1+ε)·A_t^w)]
      iv. 计算价值损失:
           L_V(φ) = ∑_{i=1}^m E_B[(V_φ^i(s_t) - G_t^i)^2]
      v. 计算熵奖励:
           L_H(θ) = -α·E_B[H(π_θ(·|s_t, w))]
      vi. 计算总损失:
           L(θ, φ) = L_π(θ) + c_V·L_V(φ) + L_H(θ)
      vii. 计算梯度:
           ∇_θ L(θ, φ), ∇_φ L(θ, φ)
      viii. 更新参数:
           θ = θ - η_π·∇_θ L(θ, φ)
           φ = φ - η_Q·∇_φ L(θ, φ)
3. 返回 θ*, φ*
</code></pre>
<p>实现细节：</p>
<ul>
<li>策略网络可以使用多层感知机(MLP)实现，输出动作概率分布</li>
<li>价值网络可以使用多头MLP实现，每个头输出一个目标的价值估计</li>
<li>目标权重采样可以使用均匀采样、高斯采样或基于Dirichlet分布的采样</li>
<li>可以使用Pareto优势函数替代简单的加权优势函数，提高多目标探索效率</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="a.1.4-gnn-morl融合算法">A.1.4 GNN-MORL融合算法</h4>
<p>GNN-MORL融合算法是将结构特征提取与优化决策结合的关键，其详细伪代码如下：</p>
<pre><code>**算法 A.4:** GNN-MORL融合算法
输入: 初始结构 G_0，GNN参数 θ_GNN，MORL参数 θ_MORL，优化步数 T，
     目标权重 w，学习率 η
输出: 优化后的结构 G*

1. 初始化当前结构 G = G_0
2. 对于 t = 0 到 T-1:
   a. // GNN特征提取
      H_node, h_graph = GNN_encoder(G; θ_GNN)
   
   b. // 状态构造
      s_t = StateConstructor(H_node, h_graph, context_t)
      其中 context_t 包含优化历史、约束条件等
   
   c. // MORL决策
      a_t = MORL_decision(s_t, w; θ_MORL)
   
   d. // 结构更新
      G' = StructureUpdater(G, a_t)
   
   e. // 性能评估
      r_t = PerformanceEvaluator(G')
      其中 r_t = [r_t^1, r_t^2, ..., r_t^m]
   
   f. // 模型更新
      如果在训练模式:
         i. 计算损失 L_t = L_MORL(r_t, s_t, a_t, w) + λ·L_GNN(G, G')
         ii. 计算梯度 ∇_θ_GNN L_t, ∇_θ_MORL L_t
         iii. 更新参数:
              θ_GNN = θ_GNN - η·∇_θ_GNN L_t
              θ_MORL = θ_MORL - η·∇_θ_MORL L_t
   
   g. 更新当前结构 G = G'
   
3. 返回优化后的结构 G* = G
</code></pre>
<p>实现细节：</p>
<ul>
<li>状态构造器可以结合GNN特征、优化历史和约束信息，构建丰富的状态表示</li>
<li>结构更新器可以实现多种更新操作，如添加/移除材料、调整密度等</li>
<li>性能评估器可以使用有限元分析或代理模型计算结构性能</li>
<li>在实际应用中，可以使用预训练模型初始化参数，加速优化过程</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="a.2-参数配置表与超参数说明">A.2 参数配置表与超参数说明</h3>
<p>本节提供了算法中使用的主要参数配置和超参数说明，以便读者复现实验结果或应用于新问题。</p>
<h4 id="a.2.1-gnn模型参数">A.2.1 GNN模型参数</h4>
<p><strong>表A.1 GNN模型参数配置</strong></p>

<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>参数名称</th>
<th>符号</th>
<th>取值</th>
<th>说明</th>

<tr>
<td>输入特征维度</td>
<td>d_in</td>
<td>8</td>
<td>节点初始特征维度，包括位置、密度、材料属性等</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>边特征维度</td>
<td>d_e</td>
<td>4</td>
<td>边特征维度，包括距离、方向、连接强度等</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>隐藏层维度</td>
<td>d_hidden</td>
<td>64</td>
<td>GNN隐藏层的特征维度</td>
</tr>

<td>GNN层数</td>
<td>L</td>
<td>3</td>
<td>图神经网络的层数</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>注意力头数</td>
<td>H</td>
<td>8</td>
<td>图注意力网络中的注意力头数量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>跳跃连接权重</td>
<td>β_3</td>
<td>0.2</td>
<td>跳跃连接的权重系数</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>激活函数</td>
<td>σ</td>
<td>ReLU</td>
<td>非线性激活函数</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dropout率</td>
<td>p_drop</td>
<td>0.1</td>

</tr>

<td>权重衰减</td>
<td>λ_GNN</td>
<td>0.0001</td>
<td>L2正则化系数</td>

<h3 id="a.3-gnn与morl相关源代码说明">A.3 GNN与MORL相关源代码说明</h3>
<p>本节提供了GNN与MORL核心模块的源代码片段，帮助读者理解算法实现细节。</p>
<h4 id="a.3.1-图构建模块">A.3.1 图构建模块</h4>
<pre class=" language-python"><code class="prism  language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> numpy <span class="token keyword">as</span> np
<span class="token keyword">import</span> networkx <span class="token keyword">as</span> nx
<span class="token keyword">from</span> scipy<span class="token punctuation">.</span>spatial <span class="token keyword">import</span> KDTree

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">build_graph_from_mesh</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>mesh_data<span class="token punctuation">,</span> k_neighbors<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
    将有限元网格转换为图结构
    
    参数:
        mesh_data: 包含单元信息的字典
            - 'elements': 单元列表
            - 'nodes': 节点坐标列表
            - 'properties': 材料属性列表
        k_neighbors: K近邻参数
        
    返回:
        G: NetworkX图对象
    """</span>
    <span class="token comment"># 初始化图</span>
    G <span class="token operator">=</span> nx<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Graph<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    <span class="token comment"># 添加节点</span>
    element_centers <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> elem <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">enumerate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>mesh_data<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'elements'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 计算单元中心</span>
        node_indices <span class="token operator">=</span> elem<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'node_indices'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        node_coords <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>mesh_data<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'nodes'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>idx<span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token keyword">for</span> idx <span class="token keyword">in</span> node_indices<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        center <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>node_coords<span class="token punctuation">,</span> axis<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 节点特征</span>
        features <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
            <span class="token string">'position'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> center<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'density'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> elem<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'density'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'young_modulus'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> elem<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'young_modulus'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'poisson_ratio'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> elem<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'poisson_ratio'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0.3</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'boundary_condition'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> elem<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'boundary_condition'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 添加节点</span>
        G<span class="token punctuation">.</span>add_node<span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">**</span>features<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        element_centers<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>center<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    <span class="token comment"># 构建KD树用于快速近邻搜索</span>
    tree <span class="token operator">=</span> KDTree<span class="token punctuation">(</span>element_centers<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    <span class="token comment"># 添加边</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>mesh_data<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'elements'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 找出相邻单元</span>
        elem <span class="token operator">=</span> mesh_data<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'elements'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        adjacent_elements <span class="token operator">=</span> elem<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'adjacent_elements'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 添加相邻连接</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> j <span class="token keyword">in</span> adjacent_elements<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> i <span class="token operator">!=</span> j <span class="token operator">and</span> <span class="token operator">not</span> G<span class="token punctuation">.</span>has_edge<span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> j<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                <span class="token comment"># 计算边特征</span>
                dist <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>linalg<span class="token punctuation">.</span>norm<span class="token punctuation">(</span>element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>j<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                direction <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>j<span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> dist
                
                <span class="token comment"># 边特征</span>
                edge_features <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
                    <span class="token string">'distance'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> dist<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'direction'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> direction<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'connection_type'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token string">'adjacent'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'weight'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">1.0</span>
                <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
                
                <span class="token comment"># 添加边</span>
                G<span class="token punctuation">.</span>add_edge<span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> j<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">**</span>edge_features<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 添加K近邻连接</span>
        _<span class="token punctuation">,</span> indices <span class="token operator">=</span> tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span>query<span class="token punctuation">(</span>element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> k<span class="token operator">=</span>k_neighbors<span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> j <span class="token keyword">in</span> indices<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>  <span class="token comment"># 排除自身</span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> i <span class="token operator">!=</span> j <span class="token operator">and</span> <span class="token operator">not</span> G<span class="token punctuation">.</span>has_edge<span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> j<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                <span class="token comment"># 计算边特征</span>
                dist <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>linalg<span class="token punctuation">.</span>norm<span class="token punctuation">(</span>element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>j<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                direction <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>j<span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> element_centers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> dist
                
                <span class="token comment"># 边特征</span>
                edge_features <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
                    <span class="token string">'distance'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> dist<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'direction'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> direction<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'connection_type'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token string">'k_nearest'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'weight'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">0.5</span>  <span class="token comment"># 长程连接权重较小</span>
                <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
                
                <span class="token comment"># 添加边</span>
                G<span class="token punctuation">.</span>add_edge<span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> j<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">**</span>edge_features<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> G
</code></pre>
<h4 id="a.3.2-gnn模型实现">A.3.2 GNN模型实现</h4>
<pre class=" language-python"><code class="prism  language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> torch
<span class="token keyword">import</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nn <span class="token keyword">as</span> nn
<span class="token keyword">import</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>functional <span class="token keyword">as</span> F
<span class="token keyword">from</span> torch_geometric<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nn <span class="token keyword">import</span> GCNConv<span class="token punctuation">,</span> GATConv<span class="token punctuation">,</span> global_mean_pool

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">HybridGNN</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Module<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
    混合GNN模型，结合GCN和GAT
    """</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> in_channels<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">,</span> out_channels<span class="token punctuation">,</span> num_layers<span class="token punctuation">,</span> heads<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> dropout<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0.1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">super</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>HybridGNN<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>num_layers <span class="token operator">=</span> num_layers
        
        <span class="token comment"># 输入投影</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>input_proj <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>in_channels<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># GCN层</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gcn_layers <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ModuleList<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>num_layers<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gcn_layers<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>GCNConv<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># GAT层</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gat_layers <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ModuleList<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>num_layers<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gat_layers<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>GATConv<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_channels <span class="token operator">//</span> heads<span class="token punctuation">,</span> heads<span class="token operator">=</span>heads<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 层归一化</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>layer_norms <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ModuleList<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>num_layers<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>layer_norms<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>LayerNorm<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 多尺度特征融合</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>fusion <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_channels <span class="token operator">*</span> num_layers<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 输出投影</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>output_proj <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_channels<span class="token punctuation">,</span> out_channels<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># Dropout</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dropout <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Dropout<span class="token punctuation">(</span>dropout<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">forward</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> edge_index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> edge_attr<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> batch<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 输入投影</span>
        h <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>input_proj<span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 存储每层的输出用于多尺度特征融合</span>
        layer_outputs <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 消息传递</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>num_layers<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token comment"># GCN传播</span>
            h_gcn <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gcn_layers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>h<span class="token punctuation">,</span> edge_index<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            
            <span class="token comment"># GAT传播</span>
            h_gat <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gat_layers<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>h<span class="token punctuation">,</span> edge_index<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            
            <span class="token comment"># 特征融合 (GCN + GAT + 跳跃连接)</span>
            h <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0.4</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> h_gcn <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">0.4</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> h_gat <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">0.2</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> h
            
            <span class="token comment"># 层归一化</span>
            h <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>layer_norms<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>h<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            
            <span class="token comment"># 非线性激活</span>
            h <span class="token operator">=</span> F<span class="token punctuation">.</span>relu<span class="token punctuation">(</span>h<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            
            <span class="token comment"># Dropout</span>
            h <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dropout<span class="token punctuation">(</span>h<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            
            <span class="token comment"># 存储层输出</span>
            layer_outputs<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>h<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 多尺度特征融合</span>
        h_multi <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>layer_outputs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        h_fused <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>fusion<span class="token punctuation">(</span>h_multi<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        h_fused <span class="token operator">=</span> F<span class="token punctuation">.</span>relu<span class="token punctuation">(</span>h_fused<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 节点特征</span>
        node_features <span class="token operator">=</span> h_fused
        
        <span class="token comment"># 图池化 (如果需要)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> batch <span class="token keyword">is</span> <span class="token operator">not</span> <span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            graph_features <span class="token operator">=</span> global_mean_pool<span class="token punctuation">(</span>node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> batch<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            graph_features <span class="token operator">=</span> node_features<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> keepdim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 输出投影</span>
        graph_features <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>output_proj<span class="token punctuation">(</span>graph_features<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> graph_features
</code></pre>
<h4 id="a.3.3-morl模型实现">A.3.3 MORL模型实现</h4>
<pre class=" language-python"><code class="prism  language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> torch
<span class="token keyword">import</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nn <span class="token keyword">as</span> nn
<span class="token keyword">import</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>functional <span class="token keyword">as</span> F
<span class="token keyword">import</span> numpy <span class="token keyword">as</span> np

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">MOPPOPolicy</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Module<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
    多目标PPO策略网络
    """</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> num_objectives<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">super</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>MOPPOPolicy<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 策略网络</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>policy_net <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Sequential<span class="token punctuation">(</span>
            nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>state_dim <span class="token operator">+</span> num_objectives<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ReLU<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ReLU<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action_dim<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 多目标价值网络</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value_nets <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ModuleList<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> _ <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>num_objectives<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            value_net <span class="token operator">=</span> nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Sequential<span class="token punctuation">(</span>
                nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>state_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ReLU<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ReLU<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Linear<span class="token punctuation">(</span>hidden_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value_nets<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>value_net<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>num_objectives <span class="token operator">=</span> num_objectives
        
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">forward</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
        前向传播
        
        参数:
            state: 状态向量
            weights: 目标权重向量
            
        返回:
            action_probs: 动作概率分布
            state_values: 状态价值估计
        """</span>
        batch_size <span class="token operator">=</span> state<span class="token punctuation">.</span>size<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 如果没有提供权重，使用均匀权重</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> weights <span class="token keyword">is</span> <span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            weights <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ones<span class="token punctuation">(</span>batch_size<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>num_objectives<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>num_objectives
        
        <span class="token comment"># 将权重与状态拼接</span>
        policy_input <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 策略网络输出</span>
        action_logits <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>policy_net<span class="token punctuation">(</span>policy_input<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        action_probs <span class="token operator">=</span> F<span class="token punctuation">.</span>softmax<span class="token punctuation">(</span>action_logits<span class="token punctuation">,</span> dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 多目标价值估计</span>
        state_values <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>num_objectives<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            value <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value_nets<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>state<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            state_values<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        state_values <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>state_values<span class="token punctuation">,</span> dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment"># [batch_size, num_objectives]</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> action_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state_values
    
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">get_action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> deterministic<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
        选择动作
        
        参数:
            state: 状态向量
            weights: 目标权重向量
            deterministic: 是否使用确定性策略
            
        返回:
            action: 选择的动作
            action_probs: 动作概率分布
            state_values: 状态价值估计
        """</span>
        action_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state_values <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>forward<span class="token punctuation">(</span>state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> deterministic<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            action <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>argmax<span class="token punctuation">(</span>action_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            action_dist <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>distributions<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Categorical<span class="token punctuation">(</span>action_probs<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            action <span class="token operator">=</span> action_dist<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sample<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state_values
    
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">evaluate_action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
        评估动作
        
        参数:
            state: 状态向量
            action: 动作
            weights: 目标权重向量
            
        返回:
            action_probs: 动作概率分布
            state_values: 状态价值估计
            action_log_probs: 动作对数概率
            entropy: 策略熵
        """</span>
        action_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state_values <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>forward<span class="token punctuation">(</span>state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        action_dist <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>distributions<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Categorical<span class="token punctuation">(</span>action_probs<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        action_log_probs <span class="token operator">=</span> action_dist<span class="token punctuation">.</span>log_prob<span class="token punctuation">(</span>action<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        entropy <span class="token operator">=</span> action_dist<span class="token punctuation">.</span>entropy<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> action_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state_values<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action_log_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> entropy
</code></pre>
<h4 id="a.3.4-gnn-morl融合实现">A.3.4 GNN-MORL融合实现</h4>
<pre class=" language-python"><code class="prism  language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> torch
<span class="token keyword">import</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nn <span class="token keyword">as</span> nn
<span class="token keyword">import</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>optim <span class="token keyword">as</span> optim

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">GNN_MORL_Fusion</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
    GNN与MORL融合框架
    """</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> gnn_model<span class="token punctuation">,</span> morl_model<span class="token punctuation">,</span> lr_gnn<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1e</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> lr_morl<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">3e</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> 
                 gnn_scale<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0.5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> morl_scale<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> clip_value<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">5.0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gnn_model <span class="token operator">=</span> gnn_model
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>morl_model <span class="token operator">=</span> morl_model
        
        <span class="token comment"># 优化器</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>optimizer_gnn <span class="token operator">=</span> optim<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Adam<span class="token punctuation">(</span>gnn_model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>parameters<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> lr<span class="token operator">=</span>lr_gnn<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>optimizer_morl <span class="token operator">=</span> optim<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Adam<span class="token punctuation">(</span>morl_model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>parameters<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> lr<span class="token operator">=</span>lr_morl<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 梯度缩放系数</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gnn_scale <span class="token operator">=</span> gnn_scale
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>morl_scale <span class="token operator">=</span> morl_scale
        
        <span class="token comment"># 梯度裁剪阈值</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip_value <span class="token operator">=</span> clip_value
        
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">optimize_step</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">,</span> actions<span class="token punctuation">,</span> rewards<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights<span class="token punctuation">,</span> next_structure_graph<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
        执行一步优化
        
        参数:
            structure_graph: 当前结构图
            actions: 执行的动作
            rewards: 获得的奖励
            weights: 目标权重
            next_structure_graph: 下一步结构图
            
        返回:
            loss: 总损失
        """</span>
        <span class="token comment"># GNN特征提取</span>
        node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> graph_features <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gnn_model<span class="token punctuation">(</span>
            structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> 
            structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>edge_index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> 
            structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>edge_attr<span class="token punctuation">,</span> 
            structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>batch
        <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 构造状态</span>
        state <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_construct_state<span class="token punctuation">(</span>node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> graph_features<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># MORL评估</span>
        _<span class="token punctuation">,</span> state_values<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action_log_probs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> entropy <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>morl_model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>evaluate_action<span class="token punctuation">(</span>
            state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> actions<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights
        <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算目标值</span>
        <span class="token keyword">with</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>no_grad<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> next_structure_graph <span class="token keyword">is</span> <span class="token operator">not</span> <span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                next_node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> next_graph_features <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gnn_model<span class="token punctuation">(</span>
                    next_structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> 
                    next_structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>edge_index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> 
                    next_structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>edge_attr<span class="token punctuation">,</span> 
                    next_structure_graph<span class="token punctuation">.</span>batch
                <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                next_state <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_construct_state<span class="token punctuation">(</span>next_node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> next_graph_features<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                _<span class="token punctuation">,</span> next_state_values<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _ <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>morl_model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>evaluate_action<span class="token punctuation">(</span>
                    next_state<span class="token punctuation">,</span> actions<span class="token punctuation">,</span> weights
                <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                next_state_values <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>zeros_like<span class="token punctuation">(</span>state_values<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算TD误差</span>
        td_error <span class="token operator">=</span> rewards <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">0.99</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> next_state_values <span class="token operator">-</span> state_values
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算价值损失</span>
        value_loss <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0.5</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>td_error <span class="token operator">**</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算策略损失</span>
        weighted_rewards <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">sum</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rewards <span class="token operator">*</span> weights<span class="token punctuation">,</span> dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> keepdim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        policy_loss <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>action_log_probs <span class="token operator">*</span> weighted_rewards<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算熵损失</span>
        entropy_loss <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">0.01</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> entropy<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算总损失</span>
        morl_loss <span class="token operator">=</span> policy_loss <span class="token operator">+</span> value_loss <span class="token operator">+</span> entropy_loss
        
        <span class="token comment"># 如果有下一步结构图，计算GNN重建损失</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> next_structure_graph <span class="token keyword">is</span> <span class="token operator">not</span> <span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            gnn_loss <span class="token operator">=</span> F<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mse_loss<span class="token punctuation">(</span>next_node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> node_features<span class="token punctuation">.</span>detach<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            gnn_loss <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tensor<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> device<span class="token operator">=</span>morl_loss<span class="token punctuation">.</span>device<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 总损失</span>
        total_loss <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>morl_scale <span class="token operator">*</span> morl_loss <span class="token operator">+</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gnn_scale <span class="token operator">*</span> gnn_loss
        
        <span class="token comment"># 梯度清零</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>optimizer_gnn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>zero_grad<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>optimizer_morl<span class="token punctuation">.</span>zero_grad<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 反向传播</span>
        total_loss<span class="token punctuation">.</span>backward<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 梯度裁剪</span>
        nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>utils<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip_grad_norm_<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gnn_model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>parameters<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip_value<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        nn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>utils<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip_grad_norm_<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>morl_model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>parameters<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip_value<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 参数更新</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>optimizer_gnn<span class="token punctuation">.</span>step<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>optimizer_morl<span class="token punctuation">.</span>step<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
            <span class="token string">'total_loss'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> total_loss<span class="token punctuation">.</span>item<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'policy_loss'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> policy_loss<span class="token punctuation">.</span>item<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'value_loss'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> value_loss<span class="token punctuation">.</span>item<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'entropy_loss'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> entropy_loss<span class="token punctuation">.</span>item<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            <span class="token string">'gnn_loss'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> gnn_loss<span class="token punctuation">.</span>item<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">_construct_state</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> node_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> graph_features<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
        构造状态表示
        """</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 这里可以根据需要自定义状态构造方法</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 简单示例: 使用图特征和节点特征的统计量</span>
        node_mean <span class="token operator">=</span> node_features<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        node_max<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _ <span class="token operator">=</span> node_features<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">max</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        state <span class="token operator">=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>graph_features<span class="token punctuation">,</span> node_mean<span class="token punctuation">,</span> node_max<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> dim<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> state
</code></pre>
